# Diatonic Modes

**Diatonic Modes: Chord Scales** 

Lydian

* Computer:   
  * \[0, 2, 4, 6, 7, 9, 11\]  
      
* Intervals:   
  * 1, 2, 3, \#4, 5, 6, 7  
      
* Triads:   
  * 1 maj, 2 maj, 3 min, \#4 dim, 5 maj, 6 min, 7 min


* 7th Chords:   
  * 1 maj7, 2 dom7, 3 min7, \#4 min7(ظآص5), 5 maj7, 6 min7, 7 min7


* 9th Chords:   
  * 1 maj9, 2 dom9, 3 min9, \#4 min7(ظآص5ظآص9), 5 maj9, 6 min9, 7 min7(ظآص9)

Ionian (Major)

* Computer:   
  * \[0, 2, 4, 5, 7, 9, 11\]


* Intervals:   
  * 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7  
      
* Triads:   
  * 1 maj, 2 min, 3 min, 4 maj, 5 maj, 6 min, 7 dim


* 7th Chords:   
  * 1 maj7, 2 min7, 3 min7, 4 maj7, 5 dom7, 6 min7, 7 min7(ظآص5)


* 9th Chords:   
  * 1 maj9, 2 min9, 3 min7(ظآص9), 4 maj9, 5 dom9, 6 min9, 7 min7(ظآص5ظآص9)

Mixolydian

* Computer:   
  * \[0, 2, 4, 5, 7, 9, 10\]  
      
* Intervals:   
  * 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, ظآص7


* Triads:   
  * 1 maj, 2 min, 3 dim, 4 maj, 5 min, 6 min, ظآص7 maj


* 7th Chords:   
  * 1 dom7, 2 min7, 3 min7(ظآص5), 4 maj7, 5 min7, 6 min7, ظآص7 maj7


* 9th Chords:   
  * 1 dom9, 2 min9, 3min7(ظآص5ظآص9), 4 maj9, 5 min9, 6 min7(ظآص9), ظآص7 maj9

Dorian

* Computer:   
  * \[0, 2, 3, 5, 7, 9, 10\]  
      
* Intervals:   
  * 1, 2, ظآص 3, 4, 5, 6, ظآص7


* Triads:   
  * 1 min, 2 min, ظآص3 maj, 4 maj, 5 min, 6 dim, ظآص7 maj


* 7th Chords:   
  * 1 min7, 2 min7, ظآص3 maj7, 4 dom7 5 min7, 6 min7(ظآص5), ظآص7 maj7


* 9th Chords:   
  * 1 min9, 2 min7(ظآص9), ظآص3 maj9, 4 dom9, 5 min9, 6 min7(ظآص5ظآص9), ظآص7 maj9

Aeolian (Minor)

* Computer:   
  * \[0, 2, 3, 5, 7, 8, 10\]  
      
* Intervals:   
  * 1, 2, ظآص3, 4, 5, ظآص6, ظآص7  
      
* Triads:  
  * 1 min, 2 min, ظآص3 maj, 4 min, 5 min, ظآص6 maj	, ظآص7 maj


* 7th Chords:   
  * 1 min7, 2 min7(ظآص5), ظآص3 maj7, 4 min7, 5 min7, ظآص6 maj7, ظآص7 dom7


* 9th Chords:   
  * 1 min9, 2 min7(ظآص5ظآص9), ظآص3 maj9, 4 min9, 5 min7(ظآص9), ظآص6 maj9, ظآص7 dom9  
    

Phrygian

* Computer:   
  * \[0, 1, 3, 5, 7, 8, 10\]  
      
* Intervals:   
  * 1, ظآص2, ظآص3, 4, 5, ظآص6, ظآص7


* Triads:   
  * 1 min, ظآص2 maj, ظآص3 maj, 4 min, 5 dim, ظآص6 maj, ظآص7 min


* 7th Chords:   
  * 1 min7, ظآص2 maj7, ظآص3 dom7, 4 min7, 5 min7(ظآص5), ظآص6 maj7, ظآص7 min7


* 9th Chords:   
  * 1 min7(ظآص9), ظآص2 maj9, ظآص3 dom9, 4 min9, 5 min7(ظآص5ظآص9), ظآص6 maj9, ظآص7 min9

Locrian

* Computer:   
  * \[0, 1, 3, 5, 6, 8, 10\]  
      
* Locrian Intervals:   
  * 1, ظآص2, ظآص3, 4, ظآص5, ظآص6, ظآص7  
      
* Triads:   
  * 1 dim, ظآص2 maj	, ظآص3 min, 4 min, ظآص5 maj,ظآص6 maj, ظآص7 min


* 7th Chords:   
  * 1 min7(ظآص5), ظآص2 maj7, ظآص3 min7, 4 min7, ظآص5 maj7, ظآص6 dom7, ظآص7 min7


* 9th Chords:   
  * 1 min7(ظآص5ظآص9), ظآص2 maj9, ظآص3 min9, 4 min7(ظآص9), ظآص5 maj9, ظآص6 dom9,ظآص7 min9

# Ionian (Major)

**C Major Scale**

\#\#\# The key of "C Major" has no sharps or flats.   
\#\#\#\# The notes of the scale are: C, D, E, F, G, A, B   
\#\#\#\# C Major Scale \= C Ionian Mode  
\_component:sequence(546ad7b7-6610-403b-8c18-5c675fa809f4, piano)\_

The notes in a scale are used to create melodies, bass lines, and chords.  
Each scale has a distinct shape, or contour, across the keyboard.

Many melodies are created from a variation on the major scale called the pentatonic scale. 

\#\#\#\# The C major pentatonic scale has 5 notes: C, D, E, G, A

# Relative Modes

**Relative Modes:**

* **Red**   
  * C Ionian, D Dorian, E Phrygian, F Lydian, G Mixolydian, A Aeolian, B Locrian   
* **Vermillion**  
  * G Ionian, A Dorian, B Phrygian, C Lydian, D Mixolydian, E Aeolian, F\# Locrian  
* **Orange**  
  * D Ionian, E Dorian, F\# Phrygian, G Lydian, A Mixolydian, B Aeolian, C\# Locrian  
* **Amber**  
  * A Ionian, B Dorian, C\# Phrygian, D Lydian, E Mixolydian, F\# Aeolian, G\# Locrian  
* **Green**  
  * E Ionian, F\# Dorian, G\# Phrygian, A Lydian, B Mixolydian, C\# Aeolian, D\# Locrian  
* **Sage**  
  * B Ionian, C\# Dorian, D\# Phrygian, E Lydian, F\# Mixolydian, G\# Aeolian, A\# Locrian  
* **Teal**  
  * F\# Ionian, G\# Dorian, A\# Phrygian, B Lydian, C\# Mixolydian, E\# Aeolian, E\# Locrian  
* **Blue**  
  * Db Ionian, Eb Dorian, F Phrygian, Gb Lydian, Ab Mixolydian, Bb Aeolian, C Locrian  
* **Indigo**  
  * Ab Ionian, Bb Dorian, C Phrygian, Db Lydian, Eb Mixolydian, F Aeolian, G Locrian  
* **Purple**  
  * Eb Ionian, F Dorian, G Phrygian, Ab Lydian, Bb Mixolydian, C Aeolian, D Locrian  
* **Magenta**  
  * Bb Ionian, C Dorian, D Phrygian, Eb Lydian, F Mixolydian, G Aeolian, A Locrian  
* **Pink**  
  * F Ionian, G Dorian, A Phrygian, Bb Lydian, C Mixolydian, D Aeolian, E Locrian

  * 1 maj7(\#5), \#2 dim7, 3 maj7, 	\#4 min7(ظآص5), \#5 min7, 6 min(maj7), 	7 dom7
